)@@G@@***    TYPE COMPUTER TO SIMPLIFY BYTE MANIPULATION.            *******  OX
)@@G@@@H@@@C. ******* 2) THE GLOBAL TAG 'BASCII' DETERMINES WHETHER INPUT     OY
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******    STRINGS ARE ASCII (=1) OR FIELDATA (=0). OZ
)@@G@@ IN THE        *******  @H@@@C. *******    CASE WHERE 2 INPUT STRINGS ARPA
)@@G@@E SPECIFIED, H1 OF         *******  @H@@@C. *******    'BASCII' REFLECTSPB
)@@G@@ THE 1ST STRING (ADDRESS IN X1)        *******  @H@@@C. *******    AND HPC
)@@G@@2 OF 'BASCII' REFLECTS THE 2ND STRING (ADDRESS     *******  @H@@@C. ****PD
)@@G@@***    IN X2).  IF H1 AND H2 ARE DIFFERENT, CONVERSION         *******  PE
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******    IS AUTOMATICALLY PERFORMED. NOTE VALUES OTHER THAN   PF
)@@G@@   *******  @H@E@C. *******    '0' OR '1' IN BASCII WILL CAUSE UNDETERMIPG
)@@G@@NED RESULSTS.  *******  @H@@@E. *******    '0' OR '1' IN BASCII WILL CAUPH
)@@G@@SE UNDETERMINED RESULTS.   *******  @H@@@C. ******* 3) BYTE NUMBERS STARPI
)@@G@@T AT 0.                                *******  @H@@@C. *******         PJ

)@@G@@@#@@@C$(1)      AXR$    @H@C@B. ****************************************RC
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@C@B. *******      BYTE MOVE SUBRORD
)@@G@@UTINE (FIELDATA)                       *******  @H@C@B. *******         RE
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@C@B. ****RF
)@@G@@***           INPUT:  X1 - INPUT BASE ADDRESS                  *******  RG
)@@G@@@H@C@B. *******                   X2 - OUTPUT BASE ADDRESS              RH
)@@G@@   *******  @H@C@B. *******                   A0 - # OF BYTES TO MOVE   RI
)@@G@@               *******  @H@C@B. *******                   A1 - BYTE # OFRJ
)@@G@@ INPUT (0-FIRST)           *******  @H@C@B. *******                   A2RK
)@@G@@ - BYTE # OF OUTPUT                    *******  @H@C@B. *******         RL
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@C@B. ****RM
)@@G@@**********************************************************************  RN
)@@G@@@^@C@BBMOVE*    +         0   @E@C@B          DS        A3,SAVE         RO
)@@G@@  . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @C@B          L         A4,A1     @^@C@B      RP
)@@G@@    SZ        A3  @G@C@B          DI,U      A3,6              . CALC WD RQ
)@@G@@# AND BYTE # OF INPUT   @ @C@B          LSSL      A4,33     @^@C@B      RR
)@@G@@    LDSL      A3,3@ @C@B          LXI,U     A3,0600001@ @C@B          L RS
)@@G@@        J0,A3     @ @C@B          L         A4,A2     @^@C@B          SZRT
)@@G@@        A3  @G@C@B          DI,U      A3,6              . CALC WD # AND RU
)@@G@@BYTE # OF OUTPUT  @ @C@B          LSSL      A4,33     @^@C@B          LDRV
)@@G@@SL      A3,3@ @C@B          LXI,U     A3,0600001@ @C@B          L       RW
)@@G@@  J1,A3     @ @C@B          L,U       SR1,0     @ @C@B          L,U     RX
)@@G@@  SR2,0     @ @C@B          L         A3,A0     @^@C@B          LSSL    RY
)@@G@@  A3,9@ @C@B          A         A3,A0     @ @C@B          LSSL      A3,1RZ
)@@G@@8     @ @C@B          L         SR3,A3    @^@C@B          BM        0,X1SA
)@@G@@@F@C@B          DL        A3,SAVE           . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    SB
)@@G@@@C@C@B          J         *BMOVE            . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@CSC
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************SD
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE MOVE SUBROUTINE                              SE
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       SF
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUTSG
)@@G@@ BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@C. *******         X2 - (SH
)@@G@@BYTE #,OUTPUT BASE ADDRESS)                  *******  @H@@@C. *******   SI
)@@G@@      A0 - # OF BYTES TO MOVE                            *******  @H@@@CSJ
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***SK
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BMOVE                   SL
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       SM
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. **********************************SN
)@@G@@****************************************  @[@@@CBMOVE*@E@@@C          DSSO
)@@G@@        A1,SBMOVE         . SAVE REGISTERS USED @A@@@C          S       SP
)@@G@@  X3,SBMOVE+2     @ @@@C          L,H1      A2,BASCII @ @@@C          L SQ
)@@G@@        A1,X1     @D@@@C          SLJ       STUFF             . GENERATESR
)@@G@@ J0   @ @@@C          L         J0,A1     @ @@@C          L,H2      A2,BSS
)@@G@@ASCII @ @@@C          L         A1,X2     @D@@@C          SLJ       STUFST
)@@G@@F             . GENERATE J1   @ @@@C          L         J1,A1     @ @@@CSU
)@@G@@          L         J2,(1*/35)@ @@@C          L,U       SR1,0     @ @@@CSV
)@@G@@          L,U       SR2,0     @ @@@C          L         A1,A0     @^@@@CSW
)@@G@@          LSSL      A1,9@ @@@C          A         A1,A0     @ @@@C      SX
)@@G@@    LSSL      A1,18     @ @@@C          L         SR3,A1    @E@@@C      SY
)@@G@@    L,H1      A1,BASCII         . GET INPUT ASCII KEY @H@@@C          L,SZ
)@@G@@U       X3,*CONVT,A1      . GET CORRESPONDING TRANSLATE TABLE     @G@@@CTA
)@@G@@          XOR,H2    A1,BASCII         . COMPARE TO OUTPUT ASCII KEY     TB
)@@G@@@H@@@C          EX        BMOVET,A2         . DO 'BM' IF KEYS =, OTHERWITC
)@@G@@SE DO 'BMT' @F@@@C          DL        A1,SBMOVE         . RESTORE REGISTTD
)@@G@@ERS USED    @A@@@C          L         X3,SBMOVE+2     @C@@@C          J TE
)@@G@@        0,X11             . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@B. ****************TF
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@@@C. ****TG
)@@G@@*** BYTE GET SUBROUTINE                                        *******  TH
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******                                                         TI
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)    TJ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - BYTE               TK
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. *******                     TL
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING TM
)@@G@@SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BGET                             *******  @H@@@C. ****TN
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  TO
)@@G@@@H@@@C. ****************************************************************TP
)@@G@@**********  @[@@@CBGET* @E@@@C          DS        A1,SBGET          . SATQ
)@@G@@VE REGISTER USED  @F@@@C          SPD       A0                . TURN ON TR
)@@G@@CHARACTER MODE    @^@@@C          OR,U      A0,1@^@@@C          LPD     TS
)@@G@@  0,A1@ @@@C          L         A2,BASCII @ @@@C          L         A1,XTT
)@@G@@1     @D@@@C          SLJ       STUFF             . GENERATE J0   @ @@@CTU
)@@G@@          S         A1,J0     @C@@@C          L,4       A0,0,*X1        TV
)@@G@@  . GET BYTE@F@@@C          SPD       A1                . TURN OFF CHARATW
)@@G@@CTER MODE   @^@@@C          AN,U      A1,1@^@@@C          LPD       0,A1TX
)@@G@@@F@@@C          DL        A1,SBGET          . RESTORE REGISTER USED     TY
)@@G@@@ @@@C          J         0,X11     @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. ****************TZ
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@C@B. ****UA
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  UB
)@@G@@@H@C@B. *******     BYTE TO INTEGER SUBROUTINE (FIELDATA)               UC
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE TO INTEGER SUBROUTINE                  UD
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@B. *******                                 UE
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #UF
)@@G@@,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@C@B. *******     INPUUG
)@@G@@T:  X1 - INPUT BASE ADDRESS                        *******  @H@C@B. ****UH
)@@G@@***             A1 - BYTE # OF INPUT STRING                    *******  UI
)@@G@@@H@C@B. *******             A0 - # OF INPUT BYTES                       UJ
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******         A0 - # OF INPUT BYTES               UK
)@@G@@               *******  @^@C@B. *******     OUTPUT: A2@H@@@C. ******* OUUL
)@@G@@TPUT: A2                                                 *******  @H@@@CUM
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***UN
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BINT                    UO
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                   J ILLEGAL-INTEGER   UP
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                   J NORMALUQ
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@B. *******               UR
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@B. **********US
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @^@C@BUT
)@@G@@BINT*     +         0   @[@@@CBINT* @E@C@B          S         A3,SAVE   UU
)@@G@@        . SAVE REGISTERS USED @E@@@C          DS        A0,SBINT        UV
)@@G@@   . SAVE REGISTERS USED@ @@@C          S         X1,SBINT+2@A@@@C      UW
)@@G@@    S         X10,SBINT+3     @G@@@C          L,U       X10,1,X11       UX
)@@G@@  . SETUP X10 FOR NORMAL RETURN     @E@@@C          SZ        NEGKEY    UY
)@@G@@        . CLEAR NEGATIVE KEY  @ @@@C          L         A2,BASCII @D@@@CUZ
)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,BGET          . GET NEXT CHAR @D@@@C          TEVA
)@@G@@        A0,NEG,A2         . IS IT '-'?    @B@@@C          J         $+4 VB
)@@G@@              . NO@F@@@C          SP1       NEGKEY            . YES, SETVC
)@@G@@ NEGATIVE KEY     @D@@@C          A         X1,(1,0)          . BUMP CHAVD
)@@G@@R PTR @D@@@C          LMJ       X11,BGET          . GET NEXT CHAR @D@@@CVE
)@@G@@          TNE       A0,ZERO,A2        . IS IT '0'?    @G@@@C          J VF
)@@G@@        BINTC1            . YES, GO TO OCTAL INTEGER LOGIC  @E@@@C      VG
)@@G@@    L         A0,SBINT          . NO, RESTORE INPUT A0@E@@@C          TZVH
)@@G@@        NEGKEY            . IS NEGATIVE KEY SET?@H@@@C          AN,U    VI
)@@G@@  A0,1              . YES, REDUCE # OF CHARS INPUT BY 1     @G@@@C      VJ
)@@G@@    J         BINTC3            . GO TO DECIMAL INTEGER LOGIC     @G@@@CVK
)@@G@@BINTC1                                . OCTAL INTEGER LOGIC FOLLOWS     VL
)@@G@@@E@@@C          DS        A3,SBINT+4        . SAVE MORE REGISTERS @ @@@CVM
)@@G@@          S         A5,SBINT+6@G@@@C          L         A3,ZERO,A2      VN
)@@G@@  . SET UP LIMITS TO TEST CHARS     @G@@@C          AN,U      A3,1      VO
)@@G@@        . CHARS MUST BE BETWEEN 0 AND 7   @A@@@C          L         A4,SVP
)@@G@@EVEN,A2     @F@@@C          SZ        A5                . BUILD BINARY VVQ
)@@G@@ALUE IN A5  @F@@@C          L         A1,SBINT          . INITIALIZE LOOVR
)@@G@@P COUNTER   @^@@@C          AN,U      A1,1@ @@@C          TZ        NEGKVS
)@@G@@EY    @^@@@C          AN,U      A1,1@E@@@CBINTL     LMJ       X11,BGET  VT
)@@G@@        . GET CHARS 1 BY 1    @G@@@C          TW        A3,A0           VU
)@@G@@  . IS CHAR BETWEEN '0' AND '7'?    @G@@@C          J         BINTC1A   VV
)@@G@@        . NO, NOT LEGAL OCTAL INTEGER     @G@@@C          AN        A0,ZVW
)@@G@@ERO,A2        . CONVERT CHARACTER TO BINARY     @G@@@C          MSI,U   VX
)@@G@@  A5,8              . MULTIPLY PREVIOUS RESULT BY 8   @D@@@C          A VY
)@@G@@        A5,A0             . ADD NEW VALUE @D@@@C          A         X1,(VZ
)@@G@@1,0)          . BUMP CHAR PTR @F@@@C          JGD       A1,BINTL        WA
)@@G@@  . IS SCAN OF FIELD COMPLETE?@H@@@C          L         A2,A5           WB
)@@G@@  . YES, A5 HAS CONVERTED OCTAL INTEGER   @ @@@C          J         BINTWC
)@@G@@C2    @G@@@CBINTC1A   AN,U      X10,1             . BAD FORMAT, SETUP FOWD
)@@G@@R BAD RETURN@F@@@CBINTC2    DL        A3,SBINT+4        . RESTORE REGISTWE
)@@G@@ERS USED    @ @@@C          L         A5,SBINT+6@F@@@C          J       WF
)@@G@@  BINTE             . GO TO NORMAL EXIT LOGIC   @ @C@B          L       WG
)@@G@@  A3,A1     @F@@@CBINTC3    L         A1,X1             . DECIMAL INTEGEWH
)@@G@@R LOGIC     @^@C@B          SZ        A2  @G@C@B          DI,U      A2,6WI
)@@G@@              . CALC WORD # AND BYTE # OF INPUT @ @C@B          LSSL    WJ
)@@G@@  A3,33     @^@C@B          LDSL      A2,3@ @C@B          LXI,U     A2,0WK
)@@G@@600001@D@@@C          SLJ       STUFF             . GENERATE J0   @ @C@BWL
)@@G@@          L         J0,A2     @ @@@C          L         J0,A1     @ @@@BWM
)@@G@@          L,U       SR1,0     @ @@@B          L,U       SR2,0     @ @@@BWN
)@@G@@          L         A2,A0     @ @@@B          LSSL      A2,27     @ @@@BWO
)@@G@@          L         SR3,A2    @ @C@B          BI        A2,0,X1   @ @@@CWP
)@@G@@          BI        A2,0,*X1  @G@C@B          TZ,H2     SR3             WQ
)@@G@@  . IF ANY ERROR OCCURRED, A2=0     @F@@@C          TZ,H2     SR3       WR
)@@G@@        . IF ANY ERROR OCCURRED,    @^@C@B          L,U       A2,0@E@@@CWS
)@@G@@          AN,U      X10,1             .   TAKE BAD RETURN   @F@C@B      WT
)@@G@@    L         A3,SAVE           . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    @E@@@CBINTE WU
)@@G@@    L         A1,A2             . IF NEGATIVE KEY SET,@E@@@C          TZWV
)@@G@@        NEGKEY            .  SET COMPLEMENT A2  @ @@@C          SN      WW
)@@G@@  A1,A2     @F@@@C          DL        A0,SBINT          . RESTORE REGISTWX
)@@G@@ERS USED    @ @@@C          L         X1,SBINT+2@ @@@C          L       WY
)@@G@@  X11,X10   @A@@@C          L         X10,SBINT+3     @C@C@B          J WZ
)@@G@@        *BINT             . RETURN  @C@@@C          J         0,X11     XA
)@@G@@        . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********************************XB
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE BLANK SUBXC
)@@G@@ROUTINE                                      *******  @H@@@C. *******   XD
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@CXE
)@@G@@. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   ***XF
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******         A0 - # OF BLANKS TO STORE                 XG
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       XH
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,XI
)@@G@@BBLANK                           *******  @H@@@C. *******               XJ
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. **********XK
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @]@@@CXL
)@@G@@BBLANK*     @E@@@C          DS        A0,SAVE           . SAVE REGISTERSXM
)@@G@@ USED @ @@@C          S         A2,SAVE+2 @F@@@C          SPD       A1  XN
)@@G@@              . TURN ON CHARACTER MODE    @^@@@C          OR,U      A1,1XO
)@@G@@@^@@@C          LPD       0,A2@ @@@C          L         A2,BASCII @ @@@CXP
)@@G@@          L         A1,X1     @D@@@C          SLJ       STUFF           XQ
)@@G@@  . GENERATE J0   @ @@@C          L         J0,A1     @^@@@C          ANXR
)@@G@@,U      A0,1@A@@@C          L         A1,BLANKS,A2    @D@@@C          S,XS
)@@G@@4       A1,0,*X1          . STORE BLANKS  @ @@@C          JGD       A0,$XT
)@@G@@-1    @F@@@C          SPD       A1                . TURN OFF CHARACTER MXU
)@@G@@ODE   @^@@@C          AN,U      A1,1@^@@@C          LPD       0,A1@F@@@CXV
)@@G@@          DL        A0,SAVE           . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    @ @@@CXW
)@@G@@          L         A2,SAVE+2 @ @@@C          J         0,X11     @[@@@CXX
)@@G@@.     @H@@@C. **********************************************************XY
)@@G@@****************  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE SEARCH SUBROUTINE                XZ
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                           YA
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (YB
)@@G@@BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@C. *******   YC
)@@G@@      A0 - SEARCH BYTE (IF=-BYTE SEARCH NOT EQUAL USED)  *******  @H@@@CYD
)@@G@@. *******         R1 - # OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING                    ***YE
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A2 - BYTE # OF FOUND BYTE                 YF
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       YG
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,YH
)@@G@@BSEARCH                          *******  @H@@@C. *******               YI
)@@G@@      J NOFIND                               *******  @H@@@C. *******   YJ
)@@G@@                  J FIND                                 *******  @H@@@CYK
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***YL
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. **********************************************************YM
)@@G@@****************  @]@@@CBSEARCH*    @E@@@C          DS        A0,SAVE   YN
)@@G@@        . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C          S         R1,SAVE+2 @F@@@CYO
)@@G@@          SPD       A1                . TURN ON CHARACTER MODE    @^@@@CYP
)@@G@@          OR,U      A1,1@^@@@C          LPD       0,A2@ @@@C          L YQ
)@@G@@        A2,BASCII @ @@@C          L         A1,X1     @D@@@C          SLYR
)@@G@@J       STUFF             . GENERATE J0   @ @@@C          L         J0,AYS
)@@G@@1     @F@@@C          L         A1,X1             . CALC # OF BYTES TO SYT
)@@G@@EARCH @ @@@C          SSL       A1,18     @ @@@C          AN        A1,RYU
)@@G@@1     @F@@@C          JP        A1,BSNO           . SKIP SEARCH IF COUNTYV
)@@G@@ <=0  @ @@@C          SN        A1,R1     @E@@@C          TN        A0  YW
)@@G@@              . IF A0<0, USE SNE    @E@@@C          J         BSC1      YX
)@@G@@        .   OTHERWISE USE SE  @ @@@C          LN        A1,A0     @ @@@CYY
)@@G@@          SNE,4     A1,0,*X1  @^@@@C          J         BSNO@^@@@C      YZ
)@@G@@    J         BSC2@E@@@CBSC1      SE,4      A0,0,*X1          . SEARCH FZA
)@@G@@OR BYTE     @C@@@C          J         BSNO              . NO FIND @F@@@CZB
)@@G@@BSC2      L         A1,J0             . CALC BYTE # OF FOUND BYTE @^@@@CZC
)@@G@@          LXI,U     A1,0@^@@@C          DSL       A1,3@ @@@C          L ZD
)@@G@@        A0,BASCII @ @@@C          MSI       A1,NBIT,A0@A@@@C          SSZE
)@@G@@L       A2,*NSHIFT,A0   @ @@@C          A         A2,A1     @^@@@C      ZF
)@@G@@    AN,U      A2,1@ @@@C          A,U       X11,1     @E@@@CBSNO      SPZG
)@@G@@D       A1                . CLEAR CHARACTER MODE@^@@@C          AN,U    ZH
)@@G@@  A1,1@^@@@C          LPD       0,A1@ @@@C          DL        A0,SAVE   ZI
)@@G@@@ @@@C          L         R1,SAVE+2 @C@@@C          J         0,X11     ZJ
)@@G@@        . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********************************ZK
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE COMPARE SZL
)@@G@@UBROUTINE                                    *******  @H@@@C. *******   ZM
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@CZN
)@@G@@. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS 1)                 ***ZO
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******         X2 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS 2)        ZP
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******         A0 - # OF BYTES TO COMPARE    ZQ
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - 0 IF 2 STRINGZR
)@@G@@S COMPARE                        *******  @H@@@C. *******               ZS
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. ******* CAZT
)@@G@@LLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BCOMP                            *******  @H@@@CZU
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***ZV
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. **********************************************************ZW
)@@G@@****************  @[@@@CBCOMP*@E@@@C          DS        A1,SBCOMP       ZX
)@@G@@  . SAVE REGISTERS USED @A@@@C          S         X2,SBCOMP+2     @A@@@CZY
)@@G@@          S         X1,SBCOMP+3     @A@@@C          S         X11,SBCOMPZZ
)@@G@@+4    @ @@@C          L,H1      A2,BASCII @F@@@C          TNE,H2    A2,BAA
)@@G@@ASCII         . IS CONVERSION IMPLIED?    @B@@@C          J         BCOMAB
)@@G@@PC            . NO@G@@@C          L,U       X2,BUFF           . CONVERT AC
)@@G@@1ST STRING INTO BUFF    @ @@@C          LMJ       X11,BMOVE @F@@@C      AD
)@@G@@    L         X11,SBCOMP+4      . RESTORE RETURN ADDRESS    @F@@@C      AE
)@@G@@    L         X1,X2             . USE BUFF FOR COMPARISON   @A@@@C      AF
)@@G@@    L         X2,SBCOMP+2     @ @@@C          L,H2      A2,BASCII @ @@@CAG
)@@G@@BCOMPC    L         A1,X1     @C@@@C          SLJ       STUFF           AH
)@@G@@  . SETUP J0@ @@@C          L         J0,A1     @ @@@C          L       AI
)@@G@@  A1,X2     @C@@@C          SLJ       STUFF             . SETUP J1@ @@@CAJ
)@@G@@          L         J1,A1     @ @@@C          L,U       SR1,0     @ @@@CAK
)@@G@@          L,U       SR2,0     @ @@@C          S         A0,A1     @^@@@CAL
)@@G@@          LSSL      A0,9@ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @ @@@C      AM
)@@G@@    LSSL      A0,18     @D@@@C          L         SR3,A0            . SEAN
)@@G@@TUP SR3     @D@@@C          BC        A0,,*X1           . BYTE COMPARE  AO
)@@G@@@F@@@C          DL        A1,SBCOMP         . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    AP
)@@G@@@A@@@C          L         X1,SBCOMP+3     @C@@@C          J         0,X1AQ
)@@G@@1             . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. ****************************AR
)@@G@@**********************************************  @C@@@C. ******* GET NEXTAS
)@@G@@ FIELD SUBROUTINE   *******   @H@@@C. ******* (FIELDS ARE DELINEATED BY AT
)@@G@@SPACES)                          *******  @H@@@C. *******               AU
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. ******* INAV
)@@G@@PUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@CAW
)@@G@@. *******         X2 - (BYTE #,OUTPUT BASE ADDRESS)                  ***AX
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******         R1 - # OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING           AY
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******         R2 - MAX # OF BYTES TO MOVE   AZ
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - # OF BYTES INBA
)@@G@@ FIELD                           *******  @H@@@C. *******         A1 - BBB
)@@G@@YTE # OF START OF FIELD                      *******  @H@@@C. *******   BC
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@CBD
)@@G@@. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,GETFIELD                         ***BE
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******                     J NOFIND                      BF
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J FIND            BG
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                           BH
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. **********************BI
)@@G@@****************************************************  @]@@@CGETFIELD*   BJ
)@@G@@@E@@@C          SZ        SFIELDKEY         . CLEAR SUBFIELD KEY  @E@@@CBK
)@@G@@          J         GETSFIELD+1       . USE GETSFIELD LOGIC @[@@@C.     BL
)@@G@@@H@@@C. ****************************************************************BM
)@@G@@**********  @H@@@C. ******* GET NEXT SUBFIELD SUBROUTINE                BN
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. ******* (SUBFIELDS ARE DELINEATED BY SPABO
)@@G@@CES OR COMMAS)             *******  @H@@@C. *******                     BP
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  BQ
)@@G@@X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@C. ****BR
)@@G@@***         X2 - (BYTE #,OUTPUT BASE ADDRESS)                  *******  BS
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******         R1 - # OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING                 BT
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******         R2 - MAX # OF BYTES TO MOVE         BU
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - # OF BYTES IN FIELDBV
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. *******         A1 - BYTE # BW
)@@G@@OF START OF FIELD                      *******  @H@@@C. *******         BX
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@C. ****BY
)@@G@@*** CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,GETSFIELD                        *******  BZ
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******                     J NOFIND                            CA
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J FIND                  CB
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. *******                                 CC
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. ****************************CD
)@@G@@**********************************************  @]@@@CGETSFIELD*  @E@@@CCE
)@@G@@          SP1       SFIELDKEY         . SET SUBFIELD KEY    @E@@@C      CF
)@@G@@    S         X11,SAVE+5        . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C          S CG
)@@G@@        A2,SAVE+3 @ @@@C          S         X1,SAVE+4 @ @@@C          S CH
)@@G@@        X3,SAVE+6 @G@@@D          L         A0,BASCII         . REVERSE CI
)@@G@@ASCII KEYS IN BASCII    @ @@@D          SSC       A0,18     @ @@@D      CJ
)@@G@@    S         A0,BASCII @E@@@D          S         A0,X3             . SACK
)@@G@@VE IN X3 ALSO     @D@D@C          L,H1      X3,BASCII         . ASCII KECL
)@@G@@Y     @A@@@C          LN        A0,SPACE,X3     @F@@@C          LMJ     CM
)@@G@@  X11,BSEARCH       . SEARCH FOR START OF FIELD @C@@@C          J       CN
)@@G@@  GETFE             . NO-FIND @G@@@C          S         A2,TEMP         CO
)@@G@@  . SAVE BYTE # OF START OF FIELD   @E@@@C          LXI       X1,A2     CP
)@@G@@        . FIND NEXT BLANK     @A@@@C          L         A0,SPACE,X3     CQ
)@@G@@@A@@@C          LMJ       X11,BSEARCH     @F@@@C          L         A2,RCR
)@@G@@1             . NO-FIND, SET TO LAST CHAR @F@@@C          L         A1,ACS
)@@G@@2             . SAVE BYTE # OF NEXT BLANK @E@@@C          L         A0,CCT
)@@G@@OMMA,X3       . FIND NEXT COMMA     @H@@@C          TZ        SFIELDKEY CU
)@@G@@        . IF SUBFIELD KEY SET, SKIP COMMA SEARCH@A@@@C          LMJ     CV
)@@G@@  X11,BSEARCH     @F@@@C          L         A2,R1             . NO-FIND,CW
)@@G@@ SET TO LAST CHAR @F@@@C          TG        A2,A1             . SET A2 TCX
)@@G@@O MIN CHAR POS    @ @@@C          L         A2,A1     @E@@@C          L CY
)@@G@@        A0,A2             . BYTE # OF ' ' OR ','@F@@@C          AN      CZ
)@@G@@  A0,TEMP           . CALC # OF BYTES TO MOVE   @E@@@C          TG      DA
)@@G@@  A0,R2             . CHECK FOR MAX SIZE  @ @@@C          L         A0,RDB
)@@G@@2     @E@@@D          L         A1,BASCII         . RESTORE ASCII KEYS  DC
)@@G@@@ @@@D          SSC       A1,18     @ @@@D          S         A1,BASCII DD
)@@G@@@E@@@C          LMJ       X11,BMOVE         . MOVE FIELD TO OUTPUT@D@@@CDE
)@@G@@          L         X11,SAVE+5        . RESTORE X11   @F@@@C          A,DF
)@@G@@U       X11,1             . POINT TO NORMAL RETURN    @ @@@C          L DG
)@@G@@        A1,TEMP   @ @@@C          AN        A2,A1     @ @@@C          L DH
)@@G@@        A0,A2     @D@@@C          J         $+2               . NORMAL RDI
)@@G@@ETURN @D@@@CGETFE     L         X11,SAVE+5        . RESTORE X11   @ @@@CDJ
)@@G@@          L         A2,SAVE+3 @ @@@C          L         X1,SAVE+4 @ @@@CDK
)@@G@@          L         X3,SAVE+6 @C@@@C          J         0,X11           DL
)@@G@@  . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. ****************************************DM
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@C. ******* FIND GIVEN FIELD SUBDN
)@@G@@ROUTINE                                *******  @H@@@C. *******         DO
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@C. ****DP
)@@G@@*** INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,BASE ADDRESS OF BLOCK)                *******  DQ
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******         X2 - (BYTE #,BASE ADDRESS OF FIELD)             DR
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******         A1 - NUMBER OF BYTES IN BLOCK       DS
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. *******         A2 - NUMBER OF BYTES IN DT
)@@G@@FIELD                      *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - BYTE # DU
)@@G@@IN BLOCK WHERE FIELD FOUND             *******  @H@@@C. *******         DV
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@C. ****DW
)@@G@@*** CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,FINDFIELD                        *******  DX
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******                     J NOFIND                            DY
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J FIND                  DZ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. *******                                 EA
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. ****************************EB
)@@G@@**********************************************  @]@@@CFINDFIELD*  @E@@@CEC
)@@G@@          S         X11,SAVE+2        . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C      ED
)@@G@@    DS        A1,SAVE+3 @ @@@C          S         X1,SAVE+5 @H@@@C      EE
)@@G@@    AN        A1,A2             . CALC # OF TIMES TO COMPARE FIELDS     EF
)@@G@@@ @@@C          S         A1,R1     @ @@@C          L         A0,A2     EG
)@@G@@@E@@@C          LMJ       X11,BCOMP         . COMPARE 2 FIELDS    @D@@@CEH
)@@G@@          JZ        A0,FINDF          . FIELD FOUND   @E@@@C          A EI
)@@G@@        X1,(1,0)          . BUMP BYTE # OF BLOCK@F@@@C          JGD     EJ
)@@G@@  R1,$-4            . CHECK FOR END OF BLOCK    @G@@@C          J       EK
)@@G@@  FINDN             . END OF BLOCK, FIELD NOT FOUND   @G@@@CFINDF     L EL
)@@G@@        A0,X1             . GET BYTE # WHERE FIELD FOUND    @ @@@C      EM
)@@G@@    SSL       A0,18     @D@@@C          L         X11,SAVE+2        . REEN
)@@G@@STORE X11   @F@@@C          A,U       X11,1             . POINT TO NORMAEO
)@@G@@L RETURN    @D@@@C          J         $+2               . NORMAL RETURN EP
)@@G@@@D@@@CFINDN     L         X11,SAVE+2        . RESTORE X11   @ @@@C      EQ
)@@G@@    DL        A1,SAVE+3 @ @@@C          L         X1,SAVE+5 @C@@@C      ER
)@@G@@    J         0,X11             . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********ES
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @H@@@CET
)@@G@@. ******* CONVERT TIME/DATE STRING TO TDATE$ FORMAT SUBROUTINE       ***EU
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* (STRINGS CAN BE OF FORM: 'HH:MM:SS' OR 'MM/DD/YY')EV
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       EW
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUTEX
)@@G@@ BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@C. *******         R1 - #EY
)@@G@@ OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING                    *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUEZ
)@@G@@TPUT: A0 - TDATE$ WORD                                   *******  @H@@@CFA
)@@G@@. *******         A1 - BYTE # AFTER FIELD                            ***FB
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******                                                   FC
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BTDATE      FD
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J ERROFE
)@@G@@R                                *******  @H@@@C. *******               FF
)@@G@@      J NORMAL                               *******  @H@@@C. *******   FG
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@CFH
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************FI
)@@G@@****  @]@@@CBTDATE*     @E@@@C          S         X11,10            . SAFJ
)@@G@@VE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C          S         X1,SBTDATE@A@@@C          DSFK
)@@G@@        A1,SBTDATE+1    @A@@@C          S         X2,SBTDATE+3    @A@@@CFL
)@@G@@          S         A3,SBTDATE+4    @D@@@C          L         A0,BASCII FM
)@@G@@        . ASCII KEY     @G@@@C          LSSL      A0,18             . SHFN
)@@G@@IFT H1 TO H2 FOR GETFIELD     @ @@@C          S         A0,BASCII @D@@@CFO
)@@G@@          SZ        TDATEA            . CLEAR OUTPUT  @E@@@C          L,FP
)@@G@@U       X2,BUFF           . EXTRACT NEXT FIELD  @^@@@C          L,U     FQ
)@@G@@  R2,8@A@@@C          LMJ       X11,GETFIELD    @D@@@C          J       FR
)@@G@@  BTDATEE+1         . NO MORE FIELDS@F@@@C          A         A0,A1     FS
)@@G@@        . CALC BYTE # AFTER FIELD   @C@@@C          S         A0,SBTDATEFT
)@@G@@+1      . SAVE    @F@@@C          L,U       A0,'/'            . IS FIELDFU
)@@G@@ DATE OR TIME?    @ @@@C          TE,S3     A0,BUFF   @C@@@C          J FV
)@@G@@        TDATET            . TIME    @D@@@C          TE,S6     A0,BUFF   FW
)@@G@@        . CHECK FORMAT  @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . FOFX
)@@G@@RMAT ERROR  @^@@@C          L,U       A2,0@ @@@C          L,U       A3,1FY
)@@G@@2     @D@@@C          L,S1      A0,BUFF           . CONVERT 'MM'  @ @@@CFZ
)@@G@@          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@CGA
)@@G@@          L,S2      A1,BUFF   @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@CGB
)@@G@@          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0           GC
)@@G@@  . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1       GD
)@@G@@  . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C          S,S1      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOGE
)@@G@@R OUTPUT    @ @@@C          L,U       A3,31     @D@@@C          L,S4    GF
)@@G@@  A0,BUFF           . CONVERT 'DD'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    GG
)@@G@@@ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S5      A1,BUFF   GH
)@@G@@@ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,A1     GI
)@@G@@@F@@@C          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    GJ
)@@G@@@D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C      GK
)@@G@@    S,S2      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @ @@@C          L,GL
)@@G@@U       A2,64     @ @@@C          L,U       A3,99     @D@@@C          L,GM
)@@G@@S1      A0,BUFF+1         . CONVERT 'YY'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'GN
)@@G@@0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S2      A1,BGO
)@@G@@UFF+1 @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,AGP
)@@G@@1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMIGQ
)@@G@@TS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @D@@@CGR
)@@G@@          AN,U      A0,64             . MODULO 64     @E@@@C          S,GS
)@@G@@S3      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @D@@@C          L       GT
)@@G@@  A0,TDATEA         . GET OUTPUT    @C@@@C          J         BTDATEE   GU
)@@G@@        . RETURN  @F@@@CTDATET    L,U       A0,':'            . CHECK FOGV
)@@G@@R FORMAT ERROR    @ @@@C          TE,S3     A0,BUFF   @D@@@C          J GW
)@@G@@        BTDATEE+1         . FORMAT ERROR  @ @@@C          TE,S6     A0,BGX
)@@G@@UFF   @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . FORMAT ERROR  @^@@@CGY
)@@G@@          LN,U      A2,1@ @@@C          L,U       A3,23     @D@@@C      GZ
)@@G@@    L,S1      A0,BUFF           . CONVERT 'HH'  @ @@@C          AN,U    HA
)@@G@@  A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S2    HB
)@@G@@  A1,BUFF   @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A       HC
)@@G@@  A0,A1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIHD
)@@G@@N LIMITS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     HE
)@@G@@@E@@@C          S,S1      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @ @@@CHF
)@@G@@          L,U       A3,59     @D@@@C          L,S4      A0,BUFF         HG
)@@G@@  . CONVERT 'MM'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSHH
)@@G@@I,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S5      A1,BUFF   @ @@@C          ANHI
)@@G@@,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C          TWHJ
)@@G@@        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C          J HK
)@@G@@        BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C          S,S2      A0,THL
)@@G@@DATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @D@@@C          L,S1      A0,BUFF+1 HM
)@@G@@        . CONVERT 'SS'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C      HN
)@@G@@    MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S2      A1,BUFF+1 @ @@@C      HO
)@@G@@    AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C      HP
)@@G@@    TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C      HQ
)@@G@@    J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @ @@@C          S,S3    HR
)@@G@@  A0,TDATEA @H@@@C          L,S1      A0,TDATEA         . CONVERT HH,MM,HS
)@@G@@SS TO SECS PAST MIDNIGHT@ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,60     @ @@@C      HT
)@@G@@    A,S2      A0,TDATEA @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,60     @ @@@C      HU
)@@G@@    A,S3      A0,TDATEA @F@@@CBTDATEE   A,U       X10,1             . POHV
)@@G@@INT TO NORMAL RETURN    @G@@@C          L         A1,BASCII         . REHW
)@@G@@STORE BASCII TO ORIGINAL VALUE@ @@@C          SSL       A1,18     @ @@@CHX
)@@G@@          S         A1,BASCII @ @@@C          L         X1,SBTDATE@A@@@CHY
)@@G@@          DL        A1,SBTDATE+1    @A@@@C          L         X2,SBTDATEHZ
)@@G@@+3    @A@@@C          L         A3,SBTDATE+4    @C@@@C          J       IA
)@@G@@  0,X10             . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********************IB
)@@G@@****************************************************  @H@@@C. ******* EXIC
)@@G@@TRACT FILE NAME STRING SUBROUTINE                        *******  @H@@@CID
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***IE
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)          IF
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******         R1 - # OF BYTES IN INPUT STRINIG
)@@G@@G                    *******  @H@@@C. *******         X2 - OUTPUT BUFFERIH
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: OUT,+1II
)@@G@@  - QUALIFIER                                *******  @H@@@C. *******   IJ
)@@G@@      OUT+2,3 - FILE-NAME                                *******  @H@@@CIK
)@@G@@. *******         OUT+4   - CYCLE (OCTAL)                            ***IL
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******         A0 = # OF BYTES IN FIELD                  IM
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******         A1 = BYTE # OF START OF FIELD IN
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                           IO
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENIP
)@@G@@CE: LMJ X11,BFILE                            *******  @H@@@C. *******   IQ
)@@G@@                  J ERROR                                *******  @H@@@CIR
)@@G@@. *******                     J NORMAL                               ***IS
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******                                                   IT
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. **********************************************IU
)@@G@@****************************  @[@@@CBFILE*@E@@@C          S         X11,IV
)@@G@@X10           . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C          S         X1,SBFILE IW
)@@G@@@A@@@C          S         X2,SBFILE+1     @A@@@C          S         X3,SIX
)@@G@@BFILE+2     @A@@@C          DS        A2,SBFILE+6     @E@@@C          L,IY
)@@G@@U       X2,BUFF           . FIND LIMITS OF FIELD@ @@@C          L,U     IZ
)@@G@@  R2,46     @A@@@C          LMJ       X11,GETFIELD    @F@@@C          J JA
)@@G@@        BFILEE+1          . NO FIELD FOUND, ERROR     @F@@@C          DSJB
)@@G@@        A0,SBFILE+4       . SAVE GETFIELD OUTPUTS     @E@@@C          A JC
)@@G@@        A0,A1             . CALC END BYTE #     @C@@@C          S       JD
)@@G@@  A0,SBFILE+3       . SAVE    @ @@@C          LXI       X1,A1     @F@@@CJE
)@@G@@          L         A3,A1             . A3 = CURRENT BYTE POINTER @D@@@CJF
)@@G@@          L         X2,SBFILE+1       . RESTORE X2    @D@@@C          L,JG
)@@G@@H1      X3,BASCII         . ASCII KEY     @E@@@C          L         A0,BJH
)@@G@@LANKS,X3      . INITIALIZE OUTPUT   @ @@@C          L         A1,A0     JI
)@@G@@@ @@@C          DS        A0,0,X2   @ @@@C          DS        A0,2,X2   JJ
)@@G@@@^@@@C          SZ        4,X2@D@@@C          L         A0,ASTER,X3     JK
)@@G@@  . SEARCH FOR '*'@A@@@C          LMJ       X11,BSEARCH     @D@@@C      JL
)@@G@@    SZ        A2                . NONE FOUND    @E@@@C          S       JM
)@@G@@  A2,QUALKEY        . SAVE BYTE # OF '*'  @D@@@C          L         A0,LJN
)@@G@@PAREN,X3      . SEARCH FOR '('@A@@@C          LMJ       X11,BSEARCH     JO
)@@G@@@D@@@C          SZ        A2                . NONE FOUND    @E@@@C      JP
)@@G@@    S         A2,CYCLEKEY       . SAVE BYTE # OF '('  @F@@@C          L JQ
)@@G@@        A0,QUALKEY        . IS THERE A QUALIFIER?     @B@@@C          JZJR
)@@G@@        A0,BFILEC         . NO@G@@@C          AN        A0,A3           JS
)@@G@@  . CALC SIZE OF QUALIFIER SUBFIELD @F@@@C          LXI,U     X2,0      JT
)@@G@@        . MOVE QUALIFIER TO OUTPUT  @ @@@C          LMJ       X11,BMOVE JU
)@@G@@@E@@@C          L         A3,QUALKEY        . BUMP A3 PAST '*'    @^@@@CJV
)@@G@@          A,U       A3,1@ @@@C          LXI       X1,A3     @E@@@CBFILECJW
)@@G@@    L         A0,CYCLEKEY       . IS THERE A CYCLE?   @^@@@C          TNJX
)@@G@@Z       A0  @E@@@C          L         A0,SBFILE+3       . NO, USE END BYJY
)@@G@@TE #  @H@@@C          AN        A0,A3             .   TO CALCULATE SIZE JZ
)@@G@@OF FILE FIELD     @ @@@C          LXI,U     X2,12     @F@@@C          LMKA
)@@G@@J       X11,BMOVE         . MOVE FILE-NAME TO OUTPUT  @F@@@C          A,KB
)@@G@@U       A3,1,A0           . BUMP A3 PAST FILE-NAME    @E@@@C          TNKC
)@@G@@Z       CYCLEKEY          . IS THERE A CYCLE?   @D@@@C          J       KD
)@@G@@  BFILEE            . NO, FINISHED  @F@@@C          LXI       X1,A3     KE
)@@G@@        . PREPARE TO EXTRACT CYCLE  @A@@@C          AN        A3,SBFILE+KF
)@@G@@3     @ @@@C          LN,XU     A0,1,A3   @F@@@C          LMJ       X11,KG
)@@G@@BINT          . CONVERT CYCLE TO BINARY   @D@@@C          J         BFILKH
)@@G@@EE+1          . FORMAT ERROR  @F@@@C          S         A2,4,X2         KI
)@@G@@  . STORE CYCLE IN OUTPUT     @G@@@CBFILEE    A,U       X10,1           KJ
)@@G@@  . GENERATE NORMAL RETURN ADDRESS  @ @@@C          L         X1,SBFILE KK
)@@G@@@A@@@C          L         X2,SBFILE+1     @A@@@C          L         X3,SKL
)@@G@@BFILE+2     @A@@@C          DL        A0,SBFILE+4     @A@@@C          DLKM
)@@G@@        A2,SBFILE+6     @C@@@C          J         0,X10             . REKN
)@@G@@TURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********************************************KO
)@@G@@****************************  @H@@@C. ******* J-REG STUFF LOCAL SUBROUTIKP
)@@G@@NE                               *******  @H@@@C. *******               KQ
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. ******* INKR
)@@G@@PUT: A1 = (BYTE #,X)                                     *******  @H@@@CKS
)@@G@@. *******        A2 = ASCII KEY                                      ***KT
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A1 = CORRESPONDING J-REG                  KU
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       KV
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. **********************************KW
)@@G@@****************************************  @^@@@CSTUFF     +         0   KX
)@@G@@@D@@@C          DS        A2,STUFFD         . SAVE A2,A3    @ @@@C      KY
)@@G@@    L         A3,A2     @ @@@C          DSL       A1,54     @ @@@C      KZ
)@@G@@    JZ        A2,STUFFC @ @@@C          DI        A1,NBIT,A3@A@@@C      LA
)@@G@@    LSSL      A2,*NSHIFT,A3   @^@@@C          LDSL      A1,3@D@@@CSTUFFCLB
)@@G@@    LXI       A1,UJ0,A3         . SET UPPER JO  @D@@@C          DL      LC
)@@G@@  A2,STUFFD         . RESTORE A2,A3 @ @@@C          J         *STUFF    LD
)@@G@@@H@@@C. ****************************************************************LE
)@@G@@**********  @^@C@BSAVE      RES       2   @[@@@C$(0)  @H@@@CBASCII*   + LF
)@@G@@        0                 . ASCII KEY (INITIALLY OFF FOR FIELDATA)@^@@@CLG
)@@G@@STUFFD    $RES      2   @^@@@CNBIT      +         6   @^@@@C          + LH

)@@G@@@^@@@CRPAREN    +         ')' @ @@@C          +         $CAS(')') @^@@@CLV
)@@G@@SAVE      $RES      7   @^@@@CSBCOMP    $RES      5   @^@@@CSBMOVE    $RLW
